===== src/hooks/use-mobile.tsx =====
import * as React from "react";

const MOBILE_BREAKPOINT = 768;

export function useIsMobile() {
  const [isMobile, setIsMobile] = React.useState<boolean | undefined>(undefined);

  React.useEffect(() => {
    const mql = window.matchMedia(`(max-width: ${MOBILE_BREAKPOINT - 1}px)`);
    const onChange = () => {
      setIsMobile(window.innerWidth < MOBILE_BREAKPOINT);
    };
    mql.addEventListener("change", onChange);
    setIsMobile(window.innerWidth < MOBILE_BREAKPOINT);
    return () => mql.removeEventListener("change", onChange);
  }, []);

  return !!isMobile;
}


===== src/lib/error-capture.ts =====
// Captures the original Error out-of-band so server.ts can recover the stack
// when h3 has already swallowed the throw into a generic 500 Response.

let lastCapturedError: { error: unknown; at: number } | undefined;
const TTL_MS = 5_000;

function record(error: unknown) {
  lastCapturedError = { error, at: Date.now() };
}

if (typeof globalThis.addEventListener === "function") {
  globalThis.addEventListener("error", (event) => record((event as ErrorEvent).error ?? event));
  globalThis.addEventListener("unhandledrejection", (event) =>
    record((event as PromiseRejectionEvent).reason),
  );
}

export function consumeLastCapturedError(): unknown {
  if (!lastCapturedError) return undefined;
  if (Date.now() - lastCapturedError.at > TTL_MS) {
    lastCapturedError = undefined;
    return undefined;
  }
  const { error } = lastCapturedError;
  lastCapturedError = undefined;
  return error;
}


===== src/lib/error-page.ts =====
export function renderErrorPage(): string {
  return `<!doctype html>
<html lang="en">
  <head>
    <meta charset="utf-8" />
    <title>This page didn't load</title>
    <meta name="viewport" content="width=device-width, initial-scale=1" />
    <style>
      body { font: 15px/1.5 system-ui, -apple-system, sans-serif; background: #fafafa; color: #111; display: grid; place-items: center; min-height: 100vh; margin: 0; padding: 1.5rem; }
      .card { max-width: 28rem; width: 100%; text-align: center; padding: 2rem; }
      h1 { font-size: 1.25rem; margin: 0 0 0.5rem; }
      p { color: #4b5563; margin: 0 0 1.5rem; }
      .actions { display: flex; gap: 0.5rem; justify-content: center; flex-wrap: wrap; }
      a, button { padding: 0.5rem 1rem; border-radius: 0.375rem; font: inherit; cursor: pointer; text-decoration: none; border: 1px solid transparent; }
      .primary { background: #111; color: #fff; }
      .secondary { background: #fff; color: #111; border-color: #d1d5db; }
    </style>
  </head>
  <body>
    <div class="card">
      <h1>This page didn't load</h1>
      <p>Something went wrong on our end. You can try refreshing or head back home.</p>
      <div class="actions">
        <button class="primary" onclick="location.reload()">Try again</button>
        <a class="secondary" href="/">Go home</a>
      </div>
    </div>
  </body>
</html>`;
}

===== src/lib/utils.ts =====
import { clsx, type ClassValue } from "clsx";
import { twMerge } from "tailwind-merge";

export function cn(...inputs: ClassValue[]) {
  return twMerge(clsx(inputs));
}


===== src/routeTree.gen.ts =====
/* eslint-disable */

// @ts-nocheck

// noinspection JSUnusedGlobalSymbols

// This file was automatically generated by TanStack Router.
// You should NOT make any changes in this file as it will be overwritten.
// Additionally, you should also exclude this file from your linter and/or formatter to prevent it from being checked or modified.

import { Route as rootRouteImport } from './routes/__root'
import { Route as PaymentRouteImport } from './routes/payment'
import { Route as JobsRouteImport } from './routes/jobs'
import { Route as ApplyRouteImport } from './routes/apply'
import { Route as IndexRouteImport } from './routes/index'

const PaymentRoute = PaymentRouteImport.update({
  id: '/payment',
  path: '/payment',
  getParentRoute: () => rootRouteImport,
} as any)
const JobsRoute = JobsRouteImport.update({
  id: '/jobs',
  path: '/jobs',
  getParentRoute: () => rootRouteImport,
} as any)
const ApplyRoute = ApplyRouteImport.update({
  id: '/apply',
  path: '/apply',
  getParentRoute: () => rootRouteImport,
} as any)
const IndexRoute = IndexRouteImport.update({
  id: '/',
  path: '/',
  getParentRoute: () => rootRouteImport,
} as any)

export interface FileRoutesByFullPath {
  '/': typeof IndexRoute
  '/apply': typeof ApplyRoute
  '/jobs': typeof JobsRoute
  '/payment': typeof PaymentRoute
}
export interface FileRoutesByTo {
  '/': typeof IndexRoute
  '/apply': typeof ApplyRoute
  '/jobs': typeof JobsRoute
  '/payment': typeof PaymentRoute
}
export interface FileRoutesById {
  __root__: typeof rootRouteImport
  '/': typeof IndexRoute
  '/apply': typeof ApplyRoute
  '/jobs': typeof JobsRoute
  '/payment': typeof PaymentRoute
}
export interface FileRouteTypes {
  fileRoutesByFullPath: FileRoutesByFullPath
  fullPaths: '/' | '/apply' | '/jobs' | '/payment'
  fileRoutesByTo: FileRoutesByTo
  to: '/' | '/apply' | '/jobs' | '/payment'
  id: '__root__' | '/' | '/apply' | '/jobs' | '/payment'
  fileRoutesById: FileRoutesById
}
export interface RootRouteChildren {
  IndexRoute: typeof IndexRoute
  ApplyRoute: typeof ApplyRoute
  JobsRoute: typeof JobsRoute
  PaymentRoute: typeof PaymentRoute
}

declare module '@tanstack/react-router' {
  interface FileRoutesByPath {
    '/payment': {
      id: '/payment'
      path: '/payment'
      fullPath: '/payment'
      preLoaderRoute: typeof PaymentRouteImport
      parentRoute: typeof rootRouteImport
    }
    '/jobs': {
      id: '/jobs'
      path: '/jobs'
      fullPath: '/jobs'
      preLoaderRoute: typeof JobsRouteImport
      parentRoute: typeof rootRouteImport
    }
    '/apply': {
      id: '/apply'
      path: '/apply'
      fullPath: '/apply'
      preLoaderRoute: typeof ApplyRouteImport
      parentRoute: typeof rootRouteImport
    }
    '/': {
      id: '/'
      path: '/'
      fullPath: '/'
      preLoaderRoute: typeof IndexRouteImport
      parentRoute: typeof rootRouteImport
    }
  }
}

const rootRouteChildren: RootRouteChildren = {
  IndexRoute: IndexRoute,
  ApplyRoute: ApplyRoute,
  JobsRoute: JobsRoute,
  PaymentRoute: PaymentRoute,
}
export const routeTree = rootRouteImport
  ._addFileChildren(rootRouteChildren)
  ._addFileTypes<FileRouteTypes>()


===== src/router.tsx =====
import { QueryClient } from "@tanstack/react-query";
import { createRouter } from "@tanstack/react-router";
import { routeTree } from "./routeTree.gen";

export const getRouter = () => {
  const queryClient = new QueryClient();

  const router = createRouter({
    routeTree,
    context: { queryClient },
    scrollRestoration: true,
    defaultPreloadStaleTime: 0,
  });

  return router;
};

  );
}

function ErrorComponent({ error, reset }: { error: Error; reset: () => void }) {
  console.error(error);
  const router = useRouter();
  return (
    <div className="flex min-h-screen items-center justify-center bg-background px-4">
      <div className="max-w-md text-center">
        <h1 className="text-xl font-semibold">This page didn't load</h1>
        <p className="mt-2 text-sm text-muted-foreground">Something went wrong. Try again or go home.</p>
        <div className="mt-6 flex flex-wrap justify-center gap-2">
          <button onClick={() => { router.invalidate(); reset(); }} className="rounded-md bg-primary px-4 py-2 text-sm font-medium text-primary-foreground hover:opacity-90">Try again</button>
          <a href="/" className="rounded-md border border-input bg-background px-4 py-2 text-sm font-medium hover:bg-accent">Go home</a>
        </div>
      </div>
    </div>
  );
}

export const Route = createRootRouteWithContext<{ queryClient: QueryClient }>()({
  head: () => ({
    meta: [
      { charSet: "utf-8" },
      { name: "viewport", content: "width=device-width, initial-scale=1" },
      { title: "Global Hire — Apply for Jobs Overseas" },
      { name: "description", content: "Apply for verified overseas jobs. Embassy-ready document submission, transparent salaries, and trusted employers in 40+ countries." },
      { property: "og:title", content: "Global Hire — Apply for Jobs Overseas" },
      { property: "og:description", content: "Apply for verified overseas jobs with embassy-ready document submission." },
      { property: "og:type", content: "website" },
      { name: "twitter:card", content: "summary_large_image" },
    ],
    links: [
      { rel: "stylesheet", href: appCss },
      { rel: "preconnect", href: "https://fonts.googleapis.com" },
      { rel: "preconnect", href: "https://fonts.gstatic.com", crossOrigin: "anonymous" },
      { rel: "stylesheet", href: "https://fonts.googleapis.com/css2?family=Inter:wght@400;500;600;700&family=Plus+Jakarta+Sans:wght@500;600;700;800&display=swap" },
    ],
  }),
  shellComponent: RootShell,
  component: RootComponent,
  notFoundComponent: NotFoundComponent,
  errorComponent: ErrorComponent,
});

function RootShell({ children }: { children: React.ReactNode }) {
  return (
    <html lang="en">
      <head><HeadContent /></head>
      <body>{children}<Scripts /></body>
    </html>
  );
}

function RootComponent() {
  const { queryClient } = Route.useRouteContext();
  return (
    <QueryClientProvider client={queryClient}>
      <Outlet />
    </QueryClientProvider>
  );
}


===== src/routes/apply.tsx =====
import { createFileRoute, Link, useNavigate } from "@tanstack/react-router";
import { useState } from "react";
import { z } from "zod";
import { getJob } from "@/lib/jobs-data";

const search = z.object({ jobId: z.string().optional() });

export const Route = createFileRoute("/apply")({
  validateSearch: (s) => search.parse(s),
  head: () => ({ meta: [{ title: "Application — Global Hire" }] }),
  component: ApplyPage,
});

const formSchema = z.object({
  fullName: z.string().trim().min(2, "Enter your full name").max(100),
  email: z.string().trim().email("Invalid email").max(255),
  phone: z.string().trim().min(6, "Enter a valid phone").max(30),
  dob: z.string().min(1, "Date of birth is required"),
  nationality: z.string().trim().min(2).max(60),
  address: z.string().trim().min(5).max(255),
  education: z.string().min(1, "Select highest education"),
  experience: z.string().trim().min(10, "Briefly describe your experience").max(1000),
});

function ApplyPage() {
  const { jobId } = Route.useSearch();
  const navigate = useNavigate();
  const job = jobId ? getJob(jobId) : undefined;

  const [form, setForm] = useState({
    fullName: "", email: "", phone: "", dob: "", nationality: "",
    address: "", education: "", experience: "",
  });
  const [errors, setErrors] = useState<Record<string, string>>({});

  if (!job) {
    return (
      <div className="min-h-screen grid place-items-center px-4">
        <div className="text-center">
          <h1 className="text-2xl font-bold">No job selected</h1>
          <p className="text-muted-foreground mt-2">Please pick a job to apply for.</p>
          <Link to="/jobs" className="mt-5 inline-block rounded-full bg-primary text-primary-foreground px-6 py-3 font-semibold">Browse jobs</Link>
        </div>
      </div>
    );
  }

  const onChange = (k: keyof typeof form) => (e: React.ChangeEvent<HTMLInputElement | HTMLSelectElement | HTMLTextAreaElement>) => {
    setForm((f) => ({ ...f, [k]: e.target.value }));
  };

  const onSubmit = (e: React.FormEvent) => {
    e.preventDefault();
    const result = formSchema.safeParse(form);
    if (!result.success) {
      const errs: Record<string, string> = {};
      result.error.issues.forEach((i) => { errs[i.path[0] as string] = i.message; });
      setErrors(errs);
      return;
    }
    setErrors({});
    try {
      sessionStorage.setItem("workabroad_application", JSON.stringify({ job: job.id, applicant: result.data }));
    } catch {}
    navigate({ to: "/payment", search: { jobId: job.id } });
  };

  const field = (label: string, name: keyof typeof form, type = "text", placeholder = "") => (
    <div>
      <label className="text-xs font-semibold uppercase tracking-wider text-muted-foreground">{label}</label>
      <input
        type={type}
        value={form[name]}
        onChange={onChange(name)}
        placeholder={placeholder}
        className="mt-1.5 w-full rounded-lg border bg-background px-3.5 py-2.5 text-sm focus:outline-none focus:ring-2 focus:ring-ring"
      />
      {errors[name] && <div className="text-xs text-[color:var(--color-destructive)] mt-1">{errors[name]}</div>}
    </div>
  );

  return (
    <div className="min-h-screen">
      <header className="sticky top-0 z-40 border-b bg-background/80 backdrop-blur">
        <nav className="max-w-6xl mx-auto px-6 h-16 flex items-center justify-between">
          <Link to="/" className="flex items-center gap-2 font-display font-extrabold text-xl">
            <span className="w-8 h-8 rounded-lg grid place-items-center text-primary-foreground" style={{ background: "var(--gradient-hero)" }}>W</span>
            Global Hire
          </Link>
          <Link to="/jobs" className="text-sm text-muted-foreground hover:text-foreground">← Back to jobs</Link>
        </nav>
      </header>

      {/* Stepper */}
      <div className="border-b bg-secondary/40">
        <div className="max-w-4xl mx-auto px-6 py-4 flex items-center gap-2 text-xs font-semibold">
          <span className="text-muted-foreground">Step 2 of 3</span>
          <div className="flex-1 h-1.5 rounded-full bg-secondary overflow-hidden">
            <div className="h-full w-2/3 rounded-full" style={{ background: "var(--gradient-hero)" }} />
          </div>
          <span>Application form</span>
        </div>
      </div>

      <section className="max-w-4xl mx-auto px-6 py-10 grid md:grid-cols-[1fr_320px] gap-8">
        <form onSubmit={onSubmit} className="rounded-2xl bg-card border p-6 md:p-8 shadow-[var(--shadow-card)] space-y-5">
          <div>
            <h1 className="text-2xl font-extrabold">Personal details</h1>
            <p className="text-sm text-muted-foreground mt-1">All information will be reviewed before embassy submission.</p>
          </div>

          <div className="grid md:grid-cols-2 gap-4">
            {field("Full name", "fullName", "text", "John Doe")}
            {field("Email address", "email", "email", "you@example.com")}
            {field("Phone number", "phone", "tel", "+1 555 000 0000")}
            {field("Date of birth", "dob", "date")}
            {field("Nationality", "nationality", "text", "e.g. Kenyan")}
            
          </div>

          {field("Home address", "address", "text", "Street, city, country")}

          <div>
            <label className="text-xs font-semibold uppercase tracking-wider text-muted-foreground">Highest education</label>
            <select
              value={form.education}
              onChange={onChange("education")}
              className="mt-1.5 w-full rounded-lg border bg-background px-3.5 py-2.5 text-sm focus:outline-none focus:ring-2 focus:ring-ring"
            >
              <option value="">Select…</option>
              <option>High School</option>
              <option>Diploma / Certificate</option>
              <option>Bachelor's Degree</option>
              <option>Master's Degree</option>
              <option>PhD</option>
            </select>
            {errors.education && <div className="text-xs text-[color:var(--color-destructive)] mt-1">{errors.education}</div>}
          </div>

          <div>
            <label className="text-xs font-semibold uppercase tracking-wider text-muted-foreground">Work experience</label>
            <textarea
              value={form.experience}
              onChange={onChange("experience")}
              rows={4}
              placeholder="Briefly describe relevant roles, employers and durations."
              className="mt-1.5 w-full rounded-lg border bg-background px-3.5 py-2.5 text-sm focus:outline-none focus:ring-2 focus:ring-ring"
            />
            {errors.experience && <div className="text-xs text-[color:var(--color-destructive)] mt-1">{errors.experience}</div>}
          </div>

          <button type="submit" className="w-full rounded-full bg-primary text-primary-foreground py-3 font-semibold hover:opacity-90 shadow-[var(--shadow-elevated)]">
            Continue to payment →
          </button>
        </form>

        <aside className="space-y-4">
          <div className="rounded-2xl bg-card border p-5 shadow-[var(--shadow-card)] sticky top-24">
            <div className="text-xs font-semibold uppercase tracking-wider text-muted-foreground">Applying for</div>
            <div className="mt-3 flex items-center gap-3">
              <div className="text-3xl">{job.flag}</div>
              <div>
                <div className="font-display font-bold">{job.title}</div>
                <div className="text-xs text-muted-foreground">{job.employer} · {job.city}</div>
              </div>
            </div>
            <div className="mt-4 space-y-2 text-sm">
              <div className="flex justify-between"><span className="text-muted-foreground">Salary / month</span><span className="font-semibold">{job.currency} {job.salaryMonth.toLocaleString()}</span></div>
              <div className="flex justify-between"><span className="text-muted-foreground">Contract</span><span className="font-semibold">{job.contractYears} yrs</span></div>
              <div className="flex justify-between"><span className="text-muted-foreground">Slots left</span><span className="font-semibold">{job.remainingSlots} / {job.totalSlots}</span></div>
            </div>
            <div className="mt-4 pt-4 border-t">
              <div className="text-xs font-semibold uppercase tracking-wider text-muted-foreground mb-2">Requirements</div>
              <ul className="text-sm space-y-1">
                {job.requirements.map((r) => (
                  <li key={r} className="flex gap-2"><span className="text-[color:var(--color-success)]">✓</span>{r}</li>
                ))}
              </ul>
            </div>
          </div>
        </aside>
      </section>
    </div>
  );
}

          <span>Licensed recruitment partner · ISO 9001 certified</span>
        </div>
      </footer>
    </div>
  );
}

function JobAlertSignup() {
  const [email, setEmail] = useState("");
  const [country, setCountry] = useState("Any country");
  const [category, setCategory] = useState("Any category");
  const [status, setStatus] = useState<"idle" | "success" | "error">("idle");

  const onSubmit = (e: React.FormEvent) => {
    e.preventDefault();
    const ok = /^[^\s@]+@[^\s@]+\.[^\s@]+$/.test(email.trim());
    if (!ok) { setStatus("error"); return; }
    setStatus("success");
    setEmail("");
  };

  return (
    <section className="border-t bg-secondary/40">
      <div className="max-w-6xl mx-auto px-6 py-20">
        <div className="relative rounded-3xl overflow-hidden border shadow-[var(--shadow-elevated)]" style={{ background: "var(--gradient-hero)" }}>
          <div className="absolute inset-0 opacity-20 mix-blend-overlay" style={{ backgroundImage: "radial-gradient(circle at 1px 1px, white 1px, transparent 0)", backgroundSize: "24px 24px" }} />

          <div className="relative grid md:grid-cols-[1.2fr_1fr] gap-8 p-8 md:p-12 text-white items-center">
            <div>
              <span className="inline-flex items-center gap-2 rounded-full bg-white/15 backdrop-blur px-3 py-1 text-xs font-semibold">
                <span className="relative flex h-2 w-2">
                  <span className="absolute inline-flex h-full w-full rounded-full bg-white opacity-75 animate-ping" />
                  <span className="relative inline-flex rounded-full h-2 w-2 bg-white" />
                </span>
                Live job alerts
              </span>
              <h2 className="mt-4 text-3xl md:text-4xl font-extrabold leading-tight">
                Get new overseas jobs in your inbox.
              </h2>
              <p className="mt-3 text-white/85 max-w-md">
                Free weekly alerts, application reminders, and visa deadlines — straight to your email. Unsubscribe anytime.
              </p>
              <div className="mt-5 flex flex-wrap gap-4 text-xs text-white/80">
                <span className="flex items-center gap-1.5">✓ Free forever</span>
                <span className="flex items-center gap-1.5">✓ No spam</span>
                <span className="flex items-center gap-1.5">✓ 28,000+ subscribers</span>
              </div>
            </div>

            <form onSubmit={onSubmit} className="rounded-2xl bg-white text-foreground p-5 shadow-[var(--shadow-elevated)] space-y-3">
              {status === "success" ? (
                <div className="text-center py-6">
                  <div className="w-12 h-12 mx-auto rounded-full grid place-items-center text-white text-xl" style={{ background: "var(--color-success)" }}>✓</div>
                  <div className="mt-3 font-display font-bold text-lg">You're subscribed!</div>
                  <p className="text-sm text-muted-foreground mt-1">Check your inbox to confirm.</p>
                  <button type="button" onClick={() => setStatus("idle")} className="mt-4 text-sm font-semibold text-primary hover:underline">Add another</button>
                </div>
              ) : (
                <>
                  <div>
                    <label className="text-xs font-semibold uppercase tracking-wider text-muted-foreground">Email address</label>
                    <input
                      type="email"
                      value={email}
                      onChange={(e) => { setEmail(e.target.value); setStatus("idle"); }}
                      placeholder="you@example.com"
                      className="mt-1.5 w-full rounded-lg border bg-background px-3.5 py-2.5 text-sm focus:outline-none focus:ring-2 focus:ring-ring"
                    />
                    {status === "error" && <div className="text-xs text-[color:var(--color-destructive)] mt-1">Please enter a valid email.</div>}
                  </div>
                  <div className="grid grid-cols-2 gap-3">
                    <div>
                      <label className="text-xs font-semibold uppercase tracking-wider text-muted-foreground">Country</label>
                      <select value={country} onChange={(e) => setCountry(e.target.value)} className="mt-1.5 w-full rounded-lg border bg-background px-2.5 py-2.5 text-sm focus:outline-none focus:ring-2 focus:ring-ring">
                        {["Any country", "Germany", "Canada", "UAE", "Saudi Arabia", "Japan", "Australia", "United Kingdom", "Singapore"].map((c) => <option key={c}>{c}</option>)}
                      </select>
                    </div>
                    <div>
                      <label className="text-xs font-semibold uppercase tracking-wider text-muted-foreground">Category</label>
                      <select value={category} onChange={(e) => setCategory(e.target.value)} className="mt-1.5 w-full rounded-lg border bg-background px-2.5 py-2.5 text-sm focus:outline-none focus:ring-2 focus:ring-ring">
                        {["Any category", "Healthcare", "Construction", "Hospitality", "Tech", "Domestic", "Logistics"].map((c) => <option key={c}>{c}</option>)}
                      </select>
                    </div>
                  </div>
                  <button type="submit" className="w-full rounded-full bg-primary text-primary-foreground py-3 font-semibold hover:opacity-90 mt-1">
                    🔔 Send me job alerts
                  </button>
                  <p className="text-[11px] text-muted-foreground text-center">By subscribing you agree to receive emails. Unsubscribe anytime.</p>
                </>
              )}
            </form>
          </div>
        </div>
      </div>
    </section>
  );
}


===== src/routes/jobs.tsx =====
import { createFileRoute, Link, useNavigate } from "@tanstack/react-router";
import { useMemo, useState } from "react";
import { ABROAD_JOBS } from "@/lib/jobs-data";

export const Route = createFileRoute("/jobs")({
  head: () => ({
    meta: [
      { title: "Browse Overseas Jobs — Global Hire" },
      { name: "description", content: "Browse verified overseas jobs by country, salary, slots and category." },
    ],
  }),
  component: JobsPage,
});

const COUNTRIES = ["All", ...Array.from(new Set(ABROAD_JOBS.map((j) => j.country)))];
const CATS = ["All", "Healthcare", "Construction", "Hospitality", "Tech", "Domestic", "Logistics"] as const;

function JobsPage() {
  const navigate = useNavigate();
  const [q, setQ] = useState("");
  const [country, setCountry] = useState("All");
  const [cat, setCat] = useState<(typeof CATS)[number]>("All");

  const jobs = useMemo(() => ABROAD_JOBS.filter((j) => {
    const m1 = q.trim() === "" || (j.title + j.employer + j.country).toLowerCase().includes(q.toLowerCase());
    const m2 = country === "All" || j.country === country;
    const m3 = cat === "All" || j.category === cat;
    return m1 && m2 && m3;
  }), [q, country, cat]);

  const apply = (id: string) => {
    navigate({ to: "/apply", search: { jobId: id } });
  };

  return (
    <div className="min-h-screen">
      <header className="sticky top-0 z-40 border-b bg-background/80 backdrop-blur">
        <nav className="max-w-6xl mx-auto px-6 h-16 flex items-center justify-between">
          <Link to="/" className="flex items-center gap-2 font-display font-extrabold text-xl">
            <span className="w-8 h-8 rounded-lg grid place-items-center text-primary-foreground" style={{ background: "var(--gradient-hero)" }}>W</span>
            Global Hire
          </Link>
          <Link to="/" className="text-sm text-muted-foreground hover:text-foreground">← Home</Link>
        </nav>
      </header>

      <section className="border-b">
        <div className="max-w-6xl mx-auto px-6 py-12">
          <h1 className="text-4xl md:text-5xl font-extrabold">Open positions abroad</h1>
          <p className="mt-3 text-muted-foreground">Choose a job, apply online and we'll submit your documents to the embassy.</p>
        </div>
      </section>

      <section className="border-b bg-secondary/40 sticky top-16 z-30 backdrop-blur">
        <div className="max-w-6xl mx-auto px-6 py-4 flex flex-wrap gap-3 items-center">
          <input
            type="search"
            value={q}
            onChange={(e) => setQ(e.target.value)}
            placeholder="Search title, employer, country…"
            className="flex-1 min-w-[220px] rounded-full bg-background border px-4 py-2.5 text-sm focus:outline-none focus:ring-2 focus:ring-ring"
          />
          <select value={country} onChange={(e) => setCountry(e.target.value)} className="rounded-full bg-background border px-4 py-2.5 text-sm font-medium">
            {COUNTRIES.map((c) => <option key={c}>{c}</option>)}
          </select>
          <select value={cat} onChange={(e) => setCat(e.target.value as (typeof CATS)[number])} className="rounded-full bg-background border px-4 py-2.5 text-sm font-medium">
            {CATS.map((c) => <option key={c}>{c}</option>)}
          </select>
        </div>
      </section>

      <section>
        <div className="max-w-6xl mx-auto px-6 py-10">
          <div className="text-sm text-muted-foreground mb-4">{jobs.length} {jobs.length === 1 ? "job" : "jobs"} available</div>
          <div className="grid md:grid-cols-2 gap-4">
            {jobs.map((j) => {
              const pct = Math.round((j.remainingSlots / j.totalSlots) * 100);
              const urgency = pct < 20 ? "text-[color:var(--color-destructive)]" : pct < 50 ? "text-amber-600" : "text-[color:var(--color-success)]";
              return (
                <div key={j.id} className="rounded-2xl bg-card border p-6 shadow-[var(--shadow-card)] hover:shadow-[var(--shadow-elevated)] transition-shadow flex flex-col">
                  <div className="flex items-start justify-between gap-3">
                    <div className="flex items-center gap-3">
                      <div className="text-3xl">{j.flag}</div>
                      <div>
                        <div className="font-display font-bold text-lg leading-tight">{j.title}</div>
                        <div className="text-xs text-muted-foreground">{j.employer}</div>
                      </div>
                    </div>
                    <span className="text-[10px] uppercase font-bold tracking-wider rounded-full bg-accent text-accent-foreground px-2.5 py-1">{j.category}</span>
                  </div>

                  <div className="mt-5 grid grid-cols-3 gap-2 text-center">
                    <div className="rounded-lg bg-secondary p-2.5">
                      <div className="text-[10px] uppercase text-muted-foreground tracking-wider">Location</div>
                      <div className="font-semibold text-sm mt-0.5">{j.city}</div>
                    </div>
                    <div className="rounded-lg bg-secondary p-2.5">
                      <div className="text-[10px] uppercase text-muted-foreground tracking-wider">Salary/mo</div>
                      <div className="font-bold text-sm mt-0.5">{j.currency} {j.salaryMonth.toLocaleString()}</div>
                    </div>
                    <div className="rounded-lg bg-secondary p-2.5">
                      <div className="text-[10px] uppercase text-muted-foreground tracking-wider">Contract</div>
                      <div className="font-semibold text-sm mt-0.5">{j.contractYears} yrs</div>
                    </div>
                  </div>

                  <div className="mt-4">
                    <div className="flex items-center justify-between text-xs">
                      <span className="text-muted-foreground">Remaining slots</span>
                      <span className={`font-bold ${urgency}`}>{j.remainingSlots} of {j.totalSlots}</span>
                    </div>
                    <div className="mt-1.5 h-1.5 rounded-full bg-secondary overflow-hidden">
                      <div className="h-full rounded-full" style={{ width: `${pct}%`, background: "var(--gradient-hero)" }} />
                    </div>
                  </div>

                  <button
                    onClick={() => apply(j.id)}
                    className="mt-5 w-full rounded-full bg-primary text-primary-foreground py-2.5 font-semibold hover:opacity-90"
                  >
                    Apply now →
                  </button>
                </div>
              );
            })}
          </div>

          {jobs.length === 0 && (
            <div className="rounded-2xl border bg-card p-12 text-center">
              <div className="font-display font-bold text-xl">No matching jobs</div>
              <div className="text-sm text-muted-foreground mt-1">Try a different filter or keyword.</div>
            </div>
          )}
        </div>
      </section>
    </div>
  );
}


===== src/routes/payment.tsx =====
import { createFileRoute, Link, useNavigate } from "@tanstack/react-router";
import { useState } from "react";
import { z } from "zod";
import { getJob } from "@/lib/jobs-data";

const search = z.object({ jobId: z.string().optional() });

export const Route = createFileRoute("/payment")({
  validateSearch: (s) => search.parse(s),
  head: () => ({ meta: [{ title: "Pay Application Fee — Global Hire" }] }),
  component: PaymentPage,
});

const APPLICATION_FEE_USD = 5;

function PaymentPage() {
  const { jobId } = Route.useSearch();
  const navigate = useNavigate();
  const job = jobId ? getJob(jobId) : undefined;

  const [card, setCard] = useState({ name: "", number: "", exp: "", cvc: "" });
  const [status, setStatus] = useState<"idle" | "processing" | "success">("idle");
  const [refId, setRefId] = useState("");

  if (!job) {
    return (
      <div className="min-h-screen grid place-items-center px-4">
        <div className="text-center">
          <h1 className="text-2xl font-bold">No application in progress</h1>
          <Link to="/jobs" className="mt-5 inline-block rounded-full bg-primary text-primary-foreground px-6 py-3 font-semibold">Browse jobs</Link>
        </div>
      </div>
    );
  }

  const formatCard = (v: string) => v.replace(/\D/g, "").slice(0, 16).replace(/(.{4})/g, "$1 ").trim();
  const formatExp = (v: string) => {
    const d = v.replace(/\D/g, "").slice(0, 4);
    return d.length > 2 ? `${d.slice(0, 2)}/${d.slice(2)}` : d;
  };

  const submit = (e: React.FormEvent) => {
    e.preventDefault();
    if (!card.name.trim() || card.number.replace(/\s/g, "").length < 12 || !card.exp || card.cvc.length < 3) return;
    setStatus("processing");
    setTimeout(() => {
      setRefId("WA-" + Date.now().toString(36).toUpperCase());
      setStatus("success");
      try { sessionStorage.removeItem("workabroad_application"); } catch {}
    }, 1500);
  };

  if (status === "success") {
    return (
      <div className="min-h-screen">
        <header className="border-b bg-background/80 backdrop-blur">
          <nav className="max-w-6xl mx-auto px-6 h-16 flex items-center">
            <Link to="/" className="flex items-center gap-2 font-display font-extrabold text-xl">
              <span className="w-8 h-8 rounded-lg grid place-items-center text-primary-foreground" style={{ background: "var(--gradient-hero)" }}>W</span>
              Global Hire
            </Link>
          </nav>
        </header>
        <section className="max-w-2xl mx-auto px-6 py-16 text-center">
          <div className="w-20 h-20 mx-auto rounded-full grid place-items-center text-3xl text-primary-foreground" style={{ background: "var(--color-success)" }}>✓</div>
          <h1 className="mt-6 text-3xl md:text-4xl font-extrabold">Application submitted!</h1>
          <p className="mt-3 text-muted-foreground">Your documents are being forwarded to the {job.country} embassy. You'll hear from us within 5–7 business days.</p>

          <div className="mt-8 rounded-2xl bg-card border p-6 shadow-[var(--shadow-card)] text-left">
            <div className="grid grid-cols-2 gap-4 text-sm">
              <div><div className="text-muted-foreground">Reference</div><div className="font-bold mt-0.5">{refId}</div></div>
              <div><div className="text-muted-foreground">Amount paid</div><div className="font-bold mt-0.5">${APPLICATION_FEE_USD}.00 USD</div></div>
              <div><div className="text-muted-foreground">Job</div><div className="font-bold mt-0.5">{job.title}</div></div>
              <div><div className="text-muted-foreground">Destination</div><div className="font-bold mt-0.5">{job.flag} {job.city}, {job.country}</div></div>
            </div>
          </div>

          <div className="mt-8 flex justify-center gap-3">
            <Link to="/jobs" className="rounded-full border px-6 py-3 font-semibold hover:bg-accent">Browse more jobs</Link>
            <Link to="/" className="rounded-full bg-primary text-primary-foreground px-6 py-3 font-semibold hover:opacity-90">Done</Link>
          </div>
        </section>
      </div>
    );
  }

  return (
    <div className="min-h-screen">
      <header className="sticky top-0 z-40 border-b bg-background/80 backdrop-blur">
        <nav className="max-w-6xl mx-auto px-6 h-16 flex items-center justify-between">
          <Link to="/" className="flex items-center gap-2 font-display font-extrabold text-xl">
            <span className="w-8 h-8 rounded-lg grid place-items-center text-primary-foreground" style={{ background: "var(--gradient-hero)" }}>W</span>
            Global Hire
          </Link>
          <Link to="/apply" search={{ jobId: job.id }} className="text-sm text-muted-foreground hover:text-foreground">← Back to form</Link>
        </nav>
      </header>

      <div className="border-b bg-secondary/40">
        <div className="max-w-4xl mx-auto px-6 py-4 flex items-center gap-2 text-xs font-semibold">
          <span className="text-muted-foreground">Step 3 of 3</span>
          <div className="flex-1 h-1.5 rounded-full bg-secondary overflow-hidden">
            <div className="h-full w-full rounded-full" style={{ background: "var(--gradient-hero)" }} />
          </div>
          <span>Payment</span>
        </div>
      </div>

      <section className="max-w-4xl mx-auto px-6 py-10 grid md:grid-cols-[1fr_320px] gap-8">
        <form onSubmit={submit} className="rounded-2xl bg-card border p-6 md:p-8 shadow-[var(--shadow-card)] space-y-5">
          <div>
            <h1 className="text-2xl font-extrabold">Pay application fee</h1>
            <p className="text-sm text-muted-foreground mt-1">A flat $5 fee covers embassy document submission.</p>
          </div>

          <div className="rounded-xl border bg-secondary/40 p-4 flex items-center justify-between">
            <div>
              <div className="text-xs uppercase tracking-wider text-muted-foreground font-semibold">Total due</div>
              <div className="text-3xl font-extrabold mt-1">${APPLICATION_FEE_USD}.00 <span className="text-sm font-medium text-muted-foreground">USD</span></div>
            </div>
            <div className="flex gap-1.5 text-2xl">💳</div>
          </div>

          <div>
            <label className="text-xs font-semibold uppercase tracking-wider text-muted-foreground">Cardholder name</label>
            <input value={card.name} onChange={(e) => setCard({ ...card, name: e.target.value })} placeholder="Name on card"
              className="mt-1.5 w-full rounded-lg border bg-background px-3.5 py-2.5 text-sm focus:outline-none focus:ring-2 focus:ring-ring" />
          </div>

          <div>
            <label className="text-xs font-semibold uppercase tracking-wider text-muted-foreground">Card number</label>
            <input value={card.number} onChange={(e) => setCard({ ...card, number: formatCard(e.target.value) })} placeholder="1234 5678 9012 3456" inputMode="numeric"
              className="mt-1.5 w-full rounded-lg border bg-background px-3.5 py-2.5 text-sm font-mono focus:outline-none focus:ring-2 focus:ring-ring" />
          </div>

          <div className="grid grid-cols-2 gap-4">
            <div>
              <label className="text-xs font-semibold uppercase tracking-wider text-muted-foreground">Expiry (MM/YY)</label>
              <input value={card.exp} onChange={(e) => setCard({ ...card, exp: formatExp(e.target.value) })} placeholder="12/28" inputMode="numeric"
                className="mt-1.5 w-full rounded-lg border bg-background px-3.5 py-2.5 text-sm font-mono focus:outline-none focus:ring-2 focus:ring-ring" />
            </div>
            <div>
              <label className="text-xs font-semibold uppercase tracking-wider text-muted-foreground">CVC</label>
              <input value={card.cvc} onChange={(e) => setCard({ ...card, cvc: e.target.value.replace(/\D/g, "").slice(0, 4) })} placeholder="123" inputMode="numeric"
                className="mt-1.5 w-full rounded-lg border bg-background px-3.5 py-2.5 text-sm font-mono focus:outline-none focus:ring-2 focus:ring-ring" />
            </div>
          </div>

          <button type="submit" disabled={status === "processing"}
            className="w-full rounded-full bg-primary text-primary-foreground py-3 font-semibold hover:opacity-90 shadow-[var(--shadow-elevated)] disabled:opacity-60">
            {status === "processing" ? "Processing payment…" : `Pay $${APPLICATION_FEE_USD}.00 & submit to embassy`}
          </button>

          <div className="text-xs text-muted-foreground text-center flex items-center justify-center gap-1.5">
            <span>🔒</span> Encrypted, PCI-compliant payment processing
          </div>
        </form>

        <aside>
          <div className="rounded-2xl bg-card border p-5 shadow-[var(--shadow-card)] sticky top-24">
            <div className="text-xs font-semibold uppercase tracking-wider text-muted-foreground">Order summary</div>
            <div className="mt-3 flex items-center gap-3">
              <div className="text-3xl">{job.flag}</div>
              <div>
                <div className="font-display font-bold">{job.title}</div>
                <div className="text-xs text-muted-foreground">{job.city}, {job.country}</div>
              </div>
            </div>
            <div className="mt-4 pt-4 border-t space-y-2 text-sm">
              <div className="flex justify-between"><span className="text-muted-foreground">Embassy submission</span><span className="font-semibold">$5.00</span></div>
              <div className="flex justify-between"><span className="text-muted-foreground">Document review</span><span className="font-semibold text-[color:var(--color-success)]">Free</span></div>
              <div className="flex justify-between"><span className="text-muted-foreground">Visa support</span><span className="font-semibold text-[color:var(--color-success)]">Free</span></div>
            </div>
            <div className="mt-4 pt-4 border-t flex justify-between font-bold">
              <span>Total</span><span>$5.00 USD</span>
            </div>
          </div>
        </aside>
      </section>
    </div>
  );
}


===== src/server.ts =====
import "./lib/error-capture";

import { consumeLastCapturedError } from "./lib/error-capture";
import { renderErrorPage } from "./lib/error-page";

type ServerEntry = {
  fetch: (request: Request, env: unknown, ctx: unknown) => Promise<Response> | Response;
};

let serverEntryPromise: Promise<ServerEntry> | undefined;

async function getServerEntry(): Promise<ServerEntry> {
  if (!serverEntryPromise) {
    serverEntryPromise = import("@tanstack/react-start/server-entry").then(
      (m) => ((m as { default?: ServerEntry }).default ?? (m as unknown as ServerEntry)),
    );
  }
  return serverEntryPromise;
}

function brandedErrorResponse(): Response {
  return new Response(renderErrorPage(), {
    status: 500,
    headers: { "content-type": "text/html; charset=utf-8" },
  });
}

function isCatastrophicSsrErrorBody(body: string, responseStatus: number): boolean {
  let payload: unknown;
  try {
    payload = JSON.parse(body);
  } catch {
    return false;
  }

  if (!payload || Array.isArray(payload) || typeof payload !== "object") {
    return false;
  }

  const fields = payload as Record<string, unknown>;
  const expectedKeys = new Set(["message", "status", "unhandled"]);
  if (!Object.keys(fields).every((key) => expectedKeys.has(key))) {
    return false;
  }

  return (
    fields.unhandled === true &&
    fields.message === "HTTPError" &&
    (fields.status === undefined || fields.status === responseStatus)
  );
}

// h3 swallows in-handler throws into a normal 500 Response with body
// {"unhandled":true,"message":"HTTPError"} — try/catch alone never fires for those.
async function normalizeCatastrophicSsrResponse(response: Response): Promise<Response> {
  if (response.status < 500) return response;
  const contentType = response.headers.get("content-type") ?? "";
  if (!contentType.includes("application/json")) return response;

  const body = await response.clone().text();
  if (!isCatastrophicSsrErrorBody(body, response.status)) {
    return response;
  }

  console.error(consumeLastCapturedError() ?? new Error(`h3 swallowed SSR error: ${body}`));
  return brandedErrorResponse();
}

export default {
  async fetch(request: Request, env: unknown, ctx: unknown) {
    try {
      const handler = await getServerEntry();
      const response = await handler.fetch(request, env, ctx);
      return await normalizeCatastrophicSsrResponse(response);
    } catch (error) {
      console.error(error);
      return brandedErrorResponse();
    }
  },
};


===== src/start.ts =====
import { createStart, createMiddleware } from "@tanstack/react-start";

import { renderErrorPage } from "./lib/error-page";

const errorMiddleware = createMiddleware().server(async ({ next }) => {
  try {
    return await next();
  } catch (error) {
    if (error != null && typeof error === "object" && "statusCode" in error) {
      throw error;
    }
    console.error(error);
    return new Response(renderErrorPage(), {
      status: 500,
      headers: { "content-type": "text/html; charset=utf-8" },
    });
  }
});

export const startInstance = createStart(() => ({
  requestMiddleware: [errorMiddleware],
}));


===== src/styles.css =====
@import "tailwindcss" source(none);
@source "../src";
@import "tw-animate-css";

===== vite.config.ts =====
// @lovable.dev/vite-tanstack-config already includes the following — do NOT add them manually
// or the app will break with duplicate plugins:
//   - tanstackStart, viteReact, tailwindcss, tsConfigPaths, cloudflare (build-only),
//     componentTagger (dev-only), VITE_* env injection, @ path alias, React/TanStack dedupe,
//     error logger plugins, and sandbox detection (port/host/strictPort).
// You can pass additional config via defineConfig({ vite: { ... } }) if needed.
import { defineConfig } from "@lovable.dev/vite-tanstack-config";

// Redirect TanStack Start's bundled server entry to src/server.ts (our SSR error wrapper).
// @cloudflare/vite-plugin builds from this — wrangler.jsonc main alone is insufficient.
export default defineConfig({
  tanstackStart: {
    server: { entry: "server" },
  },
});


===== wrangler.jsonc =====
{
  "$schema": "node_modules/wrangler/config-schema.json",
  "name": "tanstack-start-app",
  "compatibility_date": "2025-09-24",
  "compatibility_flags": ["nodejs_compat"],
  "main": "src/server.ts",
}
